name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Elegant Double Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Other
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 28, 2024
msg:I chose this hotel which was relatively close to the airport and had good reviews. I was pleasantly surprised after checking in.
The hotel, hidden among the many tea shops, has an unassuming appearance, but once you enter, it is very spacious. The two people at the front desk were very considerate and attentive:
1. The non-smoking double room requested in advance was arranged properly. It was probably upgraded to a room of more than 50 square meters when there were not many people in the off-season.
2. I wanted to know about the local snacks and places to visit around the hotel. The little sister not only introduced them in detail, but also wrote me a note with the name of the store + a hotel card.
Many tea shops outside the hotel are very commercial and not much to visit, but a lot of thought has been put into the interior of the hotel, whether it is the sunset BAR upstairs or the art leisure space on the second floor... Many succulent plants on the balcony on the top floor are very lush and cute, but The rattan basket hanging chair is old, it would be nice if we added a comfortable cushion. In the afternoon, I went to the calligraphy and painting space on the second floor to write calligraphy. It was very quiet and comfortable. The creativity of this space is really great.
As for the room, the space, facilities, layout, and hygiene are pretty good. I enjoy reading on the wide tatami. I love the big double sink and the shower facilities are very friendly. The independent bathtub is very large and looks very eye-catching. Because of the upgrade, the 1.8 large bed and duvet are very comfortable ~
The waiters I encountered in the hotel were all very nice. Everyone greeted me warmly and friendly, and responded to service needs at any time.
What I feel is inadequate is the hotel's catering. The breakfast buffet is not rich enough and the environment is very noisy (probably because it is raining and the outside is closed and there are many tourists); although there is no afternoon tea, the fruit delivered to the room is still very heart-warming.
Taking a taxi from the hotel to the scenic spot is very quick and cheap. I was not in a hurry and tried the bus. It was free, free, free, which was an unexpected surprise. Moreover, many buses can go to Sangu District in just a few stops. Sure enough, the recommendation from the little girl at the front desk was rightüëç
The best thing about the hotel is the book bar in the lobby. It has a very rich variety and a lot of new books. You can read them on the big sofa in the lobby or take them back to your room to read. Reading and writing in the hotel as you like is such a wonderful experience in a hotel in a tourist attraction. It would be perfect if the hotel could add afternoon tea and a cup of coffee.
All in all, recommended. I hope to have the opportunity to experience it again when I come to Wuyi Mountain again.
----------------------------------------

msg:The place is a little off. Although there is a riverside trail opposite, you can't walk straight there. You have to go around a long way. It's very convenient to take a taxi. It's close to the north entrance, which is suitable for going to the Dahongpao scenic area and walking on the trail in the morning.
The hotel is equipped with high-end configuration, the decoration is also high-end, and the corridor is beautiful.
As for the room, I booked it myself. The stairs are relatively narrow. I originally thought that there were toilets upstairs and downstairs, but there was only a sink downstairs, and it was made of wood and not suitable for washing faces. Later, it leaked. But the rooms here seem to be configured like this? It's a bit hard to move.
There are some minor flaws in the details of the facilities. The bedside table on the first floor is tilted. In addition, because it is a loft, the curtains are not electric and a bit difficult to pull... The bathroom is very large, with two washbasins and a bathtub, but it is specifically noted that there may be insufficient hot water if there are many people bathing at night, and there is no initiative to provide a disposable bathtub cover. So it was not used. The bed is very comfortable.
The tea provided is very delicious, Dahongpao and Zhengshan Xiaozhong. The breakfast is enough to eat, but the taste is very average.
Overall, it is a bit expensive even during the Spring Festival...
